{'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Let\'s create the error handler utility:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="frontend/src/utils/errorHandler.js">\n/**\n * Handle API errors and return a standardized error object\n * @param {Error} error - The error object from axios\n * @returns {Error} - A standardized error object with message\n */\nexport const handleApiError = (error) => {\n  let errorMessage = \'An unexpected error occurred. Please try again.\';\n  \n  if (error.response) {\n    // The request was made and the server responded with a status code\n    // that falls out of the range of 2xx\n    const { data } = error.response;\n    \n    if (data && data.message) {\n      errorMessage = data.message;\n    } else if (data && data.error) {\n      errorMessage = data.error;\n    } else if (error.response.status === 401) {\n      errorMessage = \'Authentication failed. Please log in again.\';\n    } else if (error.response.status === 403) {\n      errorMessage = \'You do not have permission to perform this action.\';\n    } else if (error.response.status === 404) {\n      errorMessage = \'The requested resource was not found.\';\n    } else if (error.response.status === 422) {\n      errorMessage = \'Validation failed. Please check your input.\';\n    } else if (error.response.status >= 500) {\n      errorMessage = \'Server error. Please try again later.\';\n    }\n  } else if (error.request) {\n    // The request was made but no response was received\n    errorMessage = \'No response from server. Please check your internet connection.\';\n  } else {\n    // Something happened in setting up the request that triggered an Error\n    errorMessage = error.message || \'An error occurred. Please try again.\';\n  }\n  \n  const customError = new Error(errorMessage);\n  customError.originalError = error;\n  return customError;\n};\n\n/**\n * Format validation errors from API response\n * @param {Object} errors - The errors object from API\n * @returns {Object} - Formatted errors object for Formik\n */\nexport const formatValidationErrors = (errors) => {\n  const formattedErrors = {};\n  \n  if (typeof errors === \'object\' && errors !== null) {\n    Object.keys(errors).forEach((key) => {\n      formattedErrors[key] = Array.isArray(errors[key]) \n        ? errors[key][0] \n        : errors[key];\n    });\n  }\n  \n  return formattedErrors;\n};\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>', 'tool_calls': None}

Please try again.\');\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleCloseTwoFactorDialog = () => {\n    setOpenTwoFactorDialog(false);\n    setTwoFactorCode(\'\');\n    setTwoFactorCodeError(\'\');\n  };\n\n  const handleEnableTwoFactor = async () => {\n    if (!twoFactorCode) {\n      setTwoFactorCodeError(\'Please enter the verification code\');\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    try {\n      setLoading(true);\n      const result = await enableTwoFactor(twoFactorCode);\n      if (result) {\n        setSuccess(\'Two-factor authentication enabled successfully!\');\n        handleCloseTwoFactorDialog();\n      }\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error(\'Error enabling two-factor authentication:\', error);\n      setTwoFactorCodeError(\'Invalid verification code. Please try again.\');\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Profile Form Validation\n  const profileValidationSchema = Yup.object({\n    firstName: Yup.string().required(\'First name is required\'),\n    lastName: Yup.string().required(\'Last name is required\'),\n    email: Yup.string().email(\'Invalid email address\').required(\'Email is required\'),\n    phoneNumber: Yup.string().required(\'Phone number is required\'),\n    dateOfBirth: Yup.date().required(\'Date of birth is required\'),\n  });\n\n  const profileFormik = useFormik({\n    initialValues: {\n      firstName: user?.firstName || \'\',\n      lastName: user?.lastName || \'\',\n      email: user?.email || \'\',\n      phoneNumber: user?.phoneNumber || \'\',\n      dateOfBirth: user?.dateOfBirth ? new Date(user.dateOfBirth) : null,\n    },\n    validationSchema: profileValidationSchema,\n    onSubmit: async (values) => {\n      try {\n        setLoading(true);\n        setError(\'\');\n        setSuccess(\'\');\n        \n        await updateProfile({\n          ...values,\n          dateOfBirth: values.dateOfBirth.toISOString(),\n        });\n        \n        setSuccess(\'Profile updated successfully!\');\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error(\'Error updating profile:\', error);\n        setError(error.message || \'Failed to update profile. Please try again.\');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    },\n  });\n\n  // Password Change Form Validation\n  const passwordChangeValidationSchema = Yup.object({\n    currentPassword: Yup.string().required(\'Current password is required\'),\n    newPassword: Yup.string()\n      .required(\'New password is required\')\n      .min(8, \'Password must be at least 8 characters\')\n      .matches(\n        /^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&])[A-Za-z\\d@$!%*?&]/,\n        \'Password must contain at least one uppercase letter, one lowercase letter, one number, and one special character\'\n      ),\n    confirmPassword: Yup.string()\n      .required(\'Please confirm your password\')\n      .oneOf([Yup.ref(\'newPassword\'), null], \'Passwords must match\'),\n  });\n\n  const passwordChangeFormik = useFormik({\n    initialValues: {\n      currentPassword: \'\',\n      newPassword: \'\',\n      confirmPassword: \'\',\n    },\n    validationSchema: passwordChangeValidationSchema,\n    onSubmit: async (values) => {\n      try {\n        setLoading(true);\n        setError(\'\');\n        setSuccess(\'\');\n        \n        await changePassword({\n          currentPassword: values.currentPassword,\n          newPassword: values.newPassword,\n        });\n        \n        setSuccess(\'Password changed successfully!\');\n        passwordChangeFormik.resetForm();\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error(\'Error changing password:\', error);\n        setError(error.message || \'Failed to change password. Please try again.\');\n      } finally {\n        setLoading(false);\n      }\n    },\n  });\n\n  // Notification Settings\n  const [notificationSettings, setNotificationSettings] = useState({\n    emailNotifications: true,\n    smsNotifications: false,\n    loginAlerts: true,\n    transactionAlerts: true,\n    marketingEmails: false,\n  });\n\n  const handleNotificationChange = (event) => {\n    setNotificationSettings({\n      ...notificationSettings,\n      [event.target.name]: event.target.checked,\n    });\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <Box>\n      <Typography variant="h4" component="h1" gutterBottom>\n        My Profile\n      </Typography>\n\n      {error && (\n        <Alert severity="error" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {error}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n\n      {success && (\n        <Alert severity="success" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>\n          {success}\n        </Alert>\n      )}\n\n      <Grid container spacing={3}>\n        <Grid item xs={12} md={4}>\n          <Card sx={{ mb: 3 </Typography>\n              <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" gutterBottom>\n                {user?.email}\n              </Typography>\n              <Button variant="outlined" React-based user interface\n\n### Technology Stack\n\n- **Backend**: Node.js with Express\n- **Frontend**: React with Material UI\n- **Database**: MongoDB\n- **Authentication**: JWT with two-factor {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Now, let\'s create a user guide for the authentication service to help users understand how to use the authentication features:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="auth-service/docs/user-guide.md">\n# QuantumMint Authentication Service User Guide\n\nThis guide provides detailed information on how to use the authentication features of the QuantumMint platform.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Introduction](#introduction)\n2. [Registration](#registration)\n3. [Email Verification](#email-verification)\n4. [Login](#login)\n5. [Two-Factor Authentication](#two-factor-authentication)\n6. [Password Management](#password-management)\n7. [User Profile](#user-profile)\n8. [Security Best Practices](#security-best-practices)\n\n## Introduction\n\nThe QuantumMint Authentication Service handles all aspects of user authentication, including registration, login, two-factor authentication, and password management. This service ensures that your account remains secure while using the QuantumMint platform.\n\n## Registration\n\n### How to Register\n\n1. Navigate to the registration page.\n2. Fill in the required information:\n   - First Name\n   - Last Name\n   - Email Address\n   - Password (must be at least 8 characters and include uppercase, lowercase, numbers, and special characters)\n   - Phone Number (optional)\n   - Date of Birth\n3. Click the "Register" button.\n4. Check your email for a verification link.\n\n### Registration API\n\n```\nPOST /api/auth/register\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "firstName": "John",\n  "lastName": "Doe",\n  "email": "john.doe@example.com",\n  "password": "Password123!",\n  "phoneNumber": "+1234567890",\n  "dateOfBirth": "1990-01-01"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Registration successful. Please check your email to verify your account."\n}\n```\n\n## Email Verification\n\nAfter registering, you\'ll receive an email with a verification link. Click on this link to verify your email address. You must verify your email before you can log in.\n\n### Email Verification API\n\n```\nGET /api/auth/verify-email/{token}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Email verified successfully. You can now log in."\n}\n```\n\n## Login\n\n### How to Login\n\n1. Navigate to the login page.\n2. Enter your email address and password.\n3. Click the "Login" button.\n4. If two-factor authentication is enabled, you\'ll be prompted to enter a verification code.\n\n### Login API\n\n```\nPOST /api/auth/login\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "john.doe@example.com",\n  "password": "Password123!"\n}\n```\n\n**Response (without 2FA):**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",\n  "user": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c85",\n    "firstName": "John",\n    "lastName": "Doe",\n    "email": "john.doe@example.com",\n    "phoneNumber": "+1234567890",\n    "role": "user",\n    "twoFactorEnabled": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response (with 2FA enabled):**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "twoFactorRequired": true,\n  "message": "Two-factor authentication required"\n}\n```\n\n## Two-Factor Authentication\n\nTwo-factor authentication (2FA) adds an extra layer of security to your account by requiring a verification code in addition to your password when logging in.\n\n### Setting Up Two-Factor Authentication\n\n1. Log in to your account.\n2. Navigate to your profile settings.\n3. Select "Security" or "Two-Factor Authentication."\n4. Click "Enable Two-Factor Authentication."\n5. Scan the QR code with an authenticator app (like Google Authenticator or Authy).\n6. Enter the verification code from your authenticator app.\n7. Save your backup codes in a secure location.\n\n### Two-Factor Authentication APIs\n\n#### Setup 2FA\n\n```\nPOST /api/2fa/setup\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "secretKey": "JBSWY3DPEHPK3PXP",\n  "qrCodeUrl": "data:image/png;base64,..."\n}\n```\n\n#### Enable 2FA\n\n```\nPOST /api/2fa/enable\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "code": "123456"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Two-factor authentication enabled successfully"\n}\n```\n\n#### Verify 2FA During Login\n\n```\nPOST /api/2fa/verify\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "john.doe@example.com",\n  "code": "123456"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",\n  "user": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c85",\n    "firstName": "John",\n    "lastName": "Doe",\n    "email": "john.doe@example.com",\n    "phoneNumber": "+1234567890",\n    "role": "user",\n    "twoFactorEnabled": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Using Backup Codes\n\nIf you lose access to your authenticator app, you can use backup codes to log in:\n\n1. On the login page, after entering your email and password, click "Use Backup Code."\n2. Enter one of your backup codes.\n3. After using a backup code, it becomes invalid. Generate new backup codes if needed.\n\n## Password Management\n\n### Forgot Password\n\nIf you forget your password, you can reset it:\n\n1. Click "Forgot Password" on the login page.\n2. Enter your email address.\n3. Check your email for a password reset link.\n4. Click the link and enter a new password.\n\n### Forgot Password APIs\n\n#### Request Password Reset\n\n```\nPOST /api/auth/forgot-password\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "email": "john.doe@example.com"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Password reset instructions sent to your email"\n}\n```\n\n#### Reset Password\n\n```\nPOST /api/auth/reset-password/{token}\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "password": "NewPassword123!",\n  "confirmPassword": "NewPassword123!"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Password reset successful. Select "Security" or "Change Password."\n3. Enter your current password and your new password.\n4. Click "Change Password."\n\n### Change Password API\n\n```\nPUT /api/users/change-password\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "currentPassword": "Password123!",\n  "newPassword": "NewPassword123!",\n  "confirmPassword": "NewPassword123!"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Password changed successfully"\n}\n```\n\n## User Profile\n\n### Viewing Your Profile\n\n1. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Now, let\'s create a user guide for the money generation service:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="money-generation/docs/user-guide.md">\n# QuantumMint Money Generation Service User Guide\n\nThis guide provides detailed information on how to use the money generation features of the QuantumMint platform.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Introduction](#introduction)\n2. [Money Generation Methods](#money-generation-methods)\n3. [Generating Money](#generating-money)\n4. [Wallet Management](#wallet-management)\n5. [Transfers](#transfers)\n6. [Deposits and Withdrawals](#deposits-and-withdrawals)\n7. [Generation History](#generation-history)\n8. [Best Practices](#best-practices)\n\n## Introduction\n\nThe QuantumMint Money Generation Service allows you to create digital money in your wallet, manage your funds, and perform various financial operations. This service is the core of the QuantumMint platform, enabling you to generate and manage your digital currency.\n\n## Money Generation Methods\n\nQuantumMint offers three different methods for generating digital money, each with its own characteristics:\n\n### Standard Generation\n\n- **Fee**: 0%\n- **Processing Time**: 24 hours\n- **Minimum Amount**: $10\n- **Maximum Amount**: $1,000\n- **KYC Required**: No\n- **Description**: The standard method is free but takes longer to process. Ideal for users who are not in a hurry and want to avoid fees.\n\n### Express Generation\n\n- **Fee**: 5%\n- **Processing Time**: 1 hour\n- **Minimum Amount**: $10\n- **Maximum Amount**: $5,000\n- **KYC Required**: Yes\n- **Description**: The express method processes your generation request faster but charges a 5% fee. Suitable for users who need funds quickly.\n\n### Premium Generation\n\n- **Fee**: 10%\n- **Processing Time**: Instant\n- **Minimum Amount**: $100\n- **Maximum Amount**: $10,000\n- **KYC Required**: Yes\n- **Description**: The premium method provides instant generation with higher limits but charges a 10% fee. Perfect for users who need immediate access to larger amounts.\n\n## Generating Money\n\n### How to Generate Money\n\n1. Log in to your QuantumMint account.\n2. Navigate to the "Generate" section.\n3. Select your preferred generation method (Standard, Express, or Premium).\n4. Enter the amount you wish to generate.\n5. Provide a purpose for the generation (e.g., "Personal expenses", "Business investment").\n6. Review the details, including any applicable fees.\n7. Confirm the generation request.\n8. Wait for the processing to complete (time varies based on the selected method).\n9. Once processed, the funds will be added to your wallet.\n\n### Generation API\n\n```\nPOST /api/generation\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "amount": 1000,\n  "method": "standard",\n  "purpose": "Personal expenses"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Generation request submitted successfully",\n  "generation": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c85",\n    "userId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c84",\n    "walletId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c83",\n    "amount": 1000,\n    "fee": 0,\n    "netAmount": 1000,\n    "method": "standard",\n    "status": "pending",\n    "purpose": "Personal expenses",\n    "createdAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Wallet Management\n\nEach user has a digital wallet that stores their generated money. You can view your wallet balance, transaction history, and perform various operations.\n\n### Viewing Your Wallet\n\n1. Log in to your QuantumMint account.\n2. Navigate to the "Wallet" section.\n3. View your current balance, wallet details, and recent transactions.\n\n### Wallet API\n\n```\nGET /api/wallets\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "wallet": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c83",\n    "userId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c84",\n    "balance": 5000,\n    "currency": "USD",\n    "type": "standard",\n    "status": "active",\n    "createdAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",\n    "updatedAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Wallet Balance\n\n```\nGET /api/wallets/balance\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "balance": 5000,\n  "formattedBalance": "$5,000.00",\n  "currency": "USD"\n}\n```\n\n## Transfers\n\nYou can transfer money from your wallet to other QuantumMint users.\n\n### How to Transfer Money\n\n1. Log in to your QuantumMint account.\n2. Navigate to the "Wallet" section.\n3. Click on "Transfer" or "Send Money."\n4. Enter the recipient\'s email address.\n5. Enter the amount you wish to transfer.\n6. Add an optional note for the recipient.\n7. Review the details and confirm the transfer.\n\n### Transfer API\n\n```\nPOST /api/wallets/transfer\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "recipientEmail": "recipient@example.com",\n  "amount": 500,\n  "note": "Payment for services"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Transfer completed successfully",\n  "transaction": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c86",\n    "senderId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c84",\n    "recipientId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c87",\n    "amount": 500,\n    "type": "transfer",\n    "status": "completed",\n    "note": "Payment for services",\n    "createdAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Deposits and Withdrawals\n\nYou can deposit money into your QuantumMint wallet from external sources or withdraw money to external accounts.\n\n### How to Deposit Money\n\n1. Log in to your QuantumMint account.\n2. Navigate to the "Wallet" section.\n3. Click on "Deposit."\n4. Select your preferred payment method.\n5. Enter the amount you wish to deposit.\n6. Follow the instructions to complete the payment.\n7. Once processed, the funds will be added to your wallet.\n\n### Deposit API\n\n```\nPOST /api/wallets/deposit\n```\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "amount": 1000,\n  "paymentMethodId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c88"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "message": "Deposit initiated successfully",\n  "transaction": {\n    "id": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c89",\n    "userId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c84",\n    "amount": 1000,\n    "type": "deposit",\n    "status": "pending",\n    "paymentMethodId": "60d21b4667d0d8992e610c88",\n    "createdAt": "2023-01-01T00:00:00.000Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### How to Withdraw Money\n\n1. Log in to your QuantumMint account.\n2. Navigate to the "Wallet" section.\n3. Click on "Withdraw."\n4. Select your preferred withdrawal method.\n5. Enter the amount you wish to withdraw.\n6. Provide the necessary account details for the withdrawal.\n7. Review the details and confirm the withdrawal.\n8. access to your wallet.\n\n6. **Provide Clear Purpose Descriptions**: When generating money, provide clear and accurate purpose descriptions to maintain a well-organized record.\n\n7. **Be Aware of following components:\n\n### Core Services\n\n1. **API Gateway**: Entry point for all client requests, handling routing, authentication verification, and request proxying\n2. **Authentication Service**: Manages user registration, login, and security\n3. **Money Generation Service**: Handles the creation and management of digital money\n4. **Transaction Service**: Processes and records all financial transactions\n5. **Payment Integration Service**: Connects with external payment providers\n6. **KYC Service**: Handles Know Your Customer verification processes\n7. **Frontend**: React-based user interface\n\n### Technology Stack\n\n- **Backend**: Node.js with Express\n- **Frontend**: React with Material UI\n- **Database**: MongoDB\n- **Authentication**: JWT with two-factor authentication\n- **Message Queue**: RabbitMQ for service communication\n- **Caching**: Redis\n- **Containerization**: Docker\n- **API Documentation**: Swagger\n\n## Features\n\n### User Management\n- User registration and authentication\n- Two-factor authentication\n- Profile management\n- Role-based access control\n\n### Money Generation\n- Multiple generation methods\n- Generation limits and controls\n- Generation history tracking\n- Wallet management\n\n### Transactions\n- Transfer between users\n- Deposit and withdrawal\n- Transaction history\n- Balance tracking\n\n### Payment Integration\n- Support for multiple payment providers\n- Secure payment processing\n- Fee calculation\n- Payment method management\n\n### KYC Verification\n- Identity verification\n- Document upload and verification\n- Verification status tracking\n- Compliance management\n\n### Security\n- JWT-based authentication\n- Two-factor authentication\n- Rate limiting\n- Input validation\n- Data encryption\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- Node.js (v14 or higher)\n- MongoDB\n- Redis\n- RabbitMQ\n- Docker (optional)\n\n### Installation\n\n1. Install dependencies for all services:\n   ```\n   npm run install-all\n   ```\n\n3. Set up environment variables:\n   - Copy `.env.example` to `.env` in each service directory\n   - Update the variables with your configuration\n\n4. Start the services:\n   ```\n   npm run start\n   ```\n\n### Using Docker\n\n1. Copy the environment variables file:\n   ```\n   cd docker\n   cp .env.example .env\n   ```\n\n2. Update the `.env` file with your configuration\n\n3. Build and start the containers:\n   ```\n   ./deploy.sh --environment dev --build\n   ```\n\n## API Documentation\n\nAPI documentation is available at `/api-docs` when the API Gateway is running. Payment integration service\n├── kyc-service/            # KYC verification service\n├── frontend/               # React frontend application\n├── docker/                 # Docker configuration files\n└── shared/                 # Shared utilities and models\n```\n\n### Running Individual Services\n\nEach service can be run independently for development:\n\n```\ncd <service-directory>\nnpm run dev\n```\n\nThis will start the service in development mode with hot reloading.\n\n### Testing\n\nRun tests for all services:\n\n```\nnpm test\n```\n\nOr for a specific service:\n\n```\ncd <service-directory>\nnpm test\n```\n\n## Deployment\n\nThe application can be deployed using Docker and Docker Compose:\n\n```\ncd docker\n./deploy.sh --environment prod --build\n```\n\n## CI/CD Pipeline\n\nThe project includes a GitHub Actions workflow for continuous integration and deployment:\n\n1. **Testing**: Runs linting and unit tests for each service\n2. **Building**: Builds Docker images for each service\n3. **Deployment**: Deploys to staging or production environments based on the branch\n\n## Documentation\n\n- User guides are available in the `docs` directory of each service\n- API documentation is available at `/api-docs` when the API Gateway is running\n- Technical documentation is available in the `docs` directory of the project\n\n## License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License - see the LICENSE file for details.\n\n## Acknowledgments\n\n- The NinjaTech AI team for their support and guidance\n- All contributors to the project\n</full-file-rewrite>\n</function_calls>', 'tool_calls': None}
